decoded_image = base64.b64decode(embedded_image)

img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(decoded_image))

img_tk = ImageTk.PhotoImage(img)

label = tk.Label(popup, image=img_tk)

label.pack()

def on_close():

popup.destroy()

create_popup()

popup.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", on_close)

popup.mainloop()
